Plates were washed with PBS and incubated 2 hours at 37°C with a mixture of anti-CD3 (3 μg/ml, clone Hit3a, BD Biosciences) and 20 μg/ml Delta1-Fc or hIgG4 control (Sigma). Plates were again washed with PBS and purified CD4+ T cells were seeded at 2 × 105/well in the presence of soluble anti-CD28 (2 μg/ml, clone CD28.2, BD Bioscience).">
